    </a>
    <h4>Gemma Guard — Android phishing detection with on-device Gemma 4</h4>
    <p>Android app that captures the screen, runs OCR, and uses Gemma 4 locally to detect and explain phishing risks before users tap.

Gemma Guard was built for the Google Gemma 4 Good Hackathon as a privacy-first Android app that shows how Gemma can be used in a real mobile safety workflow: capture a risky screen, reason locally, explain the result, and help the user act safely.</p>
    <a href="https://thataicollection.com/redirect/gemma-guard" target="_blank"><b>Get Started with Gemma Guard</b></a>
